Shanxi Generals Arrive in Shenyang

Song Zheyuan, Fu Zuoyi, Sun Chu, and Zhou Dai All Spoke

Shenyang Dispatch: Shanxi generals, Army Commander Fu Zuoyi, Division Commanders Li Fuying, Yang Yaofang, and Feng Pengzhu; Road Protection Commander Sun Chu; Artillery Training Supervisor Zhou Dai; and Liu Zhaotang, representative of Army Commander Yang Aiyuan, all arrived in the east by the Beining Railway night express train from Tianjin on the evening of the 8th. In addition, Army Commander Song Zheyuan of the Third Army, along with former Shaanxi Provincial Government Chairman Men Zhizhong, also arrived on the same train. The train arrived at Shenyang Liaoning Main Station at about 9 PM on the 9th. Deputy Commander Zhang had received a telegram from Pingjin in advance and ordered the Adjutant Office of the Frontier Defense Headquarters to prepare for the reception and sent Yang Zhengzhi, the director of the Adjutant Office, as a representative to the station to welcome them. When Fu and others arrived at Shenyang Station that day, Yang, together with Guo Fuhuan, the head of the Public Relations Section of the Deputy Civil Affairs Office, and various adjutants, went to receive them. Pang Bingxun, the commander of the Independent First Division, who had come to Shenyang to pay his respects to Zhang but had not yet returned; Rong Honglu, the commander of the Jin Garrison; Zhao Chengshou, the supervisor of the Jin Cavalry; and Bao Wenwei, the newly appointed Deputy Chief of the General Staff; and Ji Yiqiao and Fu Zhan Kui, two commissioners sent by the Northeast to inspect the Jin Army (Fu returned to Shenyang the day before), and those who had friendly relations with Fu, Song, etc., all went to the station to welcome them. After the generals got off the train and exchanged greetings with the welcoming personnel, they dispersed. Fu Zuoyi stayed at the Liaoning Hotel in the commercial area, Li Fuying stayed at the Lingge Hotel on Sanjing Road, and Sun Chu, Zhou Dai, Feng Pengzhu, Yang Yaofang, Liu Zhaotang, the representative of Yang Aiyuan, etc., all stayed at the Frontier Defense Headquarters Reception Office on Sanjing Road. Song Zheyuan and Men Zhizhong stayed at the Liaoning Office of the Third Army. Song's staff officer, Qin Shaowen, also came with Zhu. Song had previously established a Liaoning Office in Shenyang, and the representative in Shenyang was Bai Fengyi. At 9:30 AM today (the 10th), Song was summoned by Deputy Commander Zhang and talked for about an hour. At noon, reporters visited Song at his office. According to him, he was summoned by Deputy Commander Zhang to come from Shanxi to Tianjin. Because he caught a cold on the way, his health was not good, so he stayed in Tianjin for two days. He did not come with Commander Fu and others from Tianjin until the night of the 8th. At 9:30 this morning, he was invited by the Deputy Commander to inquire about the organization of his army and discuss the method of giving salary in the future in detail. Regarding the organization of the Third Army, it should follow the Deputy Commander's instructions and decide based on the financial situation. The Deputy Commander agreed that the salary would be allocated by the Northeast, and the method could be determined within a few days. He originally planned to stay in Shenyang for a week, but the Deputy Commander asked him to stay for a few more days and ordered him to visit the Ordnance Factory and the Aviation Command. Regarding the fact that Yang's troops of the Jin Army were stationed in Fenyang, it was due to a misunderstanding by lower-level officers and soldiers, which has now been explained and there is nothing to worry about. Finally, when asked about Feng's going abroad, Song replied that Feng's going abroad would depend on whether the central government issued a strict order to urge him. He did not hear anything else. At 5 PM that afternoon, the reporter visited Fu Zuoyi at the Liaoning Hotel again. According to Fu, the army commanders, division commanders, and commanders of Shanxi came to Shenyang to pay their respects to Deputy Commander Zhang and report on the reorganization of their troops and the recent situation in Shanxi. Because they had been ordered to be under the command of Deputy Commander Zhang, they should pay their respects and ask for instructions. There were no other tasks besides these three points. Feng's going abroad is what the Chinese people hope for, and Feng himself also intends to go abroad and is discussing the procedures with Shanxi. At present, the troops stationed in Shanxi are all national troops and there is no difference. However, there are too many troops stationed in Shanxi. In order to reduce the burden on the people of Shanxi, it is hoped that the troops will be transferred in the future. As for the fall in Jin banknotes, it has greatly affected the livelihood of the people of Shanxi. Although the provincial government now draws lots every month to cash out 500,000 yuan per month, according to the total number of issues, which is more than 60 million, it will take ten years to clear it. Therefore, the people of Shanxi hope that the central government and Deputy Commander Zhang will find a way to provide relief and approve the early issuance of the Jin Banknote Financial Public Bonds, or they must find another way. He will stay in Shenyang for about a week and then return to his defense. Chairman Shang is unable to come to Shenyang for a while, and Shang has sent a representative, Lu Xian, to Shenyang. Commander Zhao (Chengshou) will return to his defense soon. The reporter also visited Sun Chu and Zhou Dai at the Frontier Defense Headquarters Reception Office. According to Zhou Dai, the troops under his command have been reorganized into ten regiments, each with thirty-six cannons. The organization is the same as that of the Northeast, and the two inspectors, Ji and Fu, have completed the inspection. They are currently stationed in Taiyuan, accounting for half of the total number, and the remaining half are suppressing bandits in the border area of ​​Suiyuan and stationed in the Jinan area. This trip is to pay respects to the Deputy Commander, report and ask for instructions. After staying for a few days, he will return to his defense to reorganize the troops. Sun Chu said that Deputy Commander Zhang had previously telegraphed to invite Chairman Shang to Shenyang, but Shang had to wait for the cleanup due to the accumulation of Jin politics and would not come to Shenyang for the time being. He will visit Zhang and visit various military agencies before returning to his defense, and Commander Fu may have to stay for a few more days. The five people, including Sun Chu, visited the heads of various departments and offices of the Frontier Defense Headquarters at 10 AM on the morning of the 10th. At 6 PM in the evening, they met with Fu Zuoyi to pay their respects to Deputy Commander Zhang. Pang Bingxun has received 40,000 yuan in supplies and will return to his defense with Song Zheyuan. The heads of the Frontier Defense Headquarters and the generals of the Northwest Army gathered in Shenyang. Deputy Commander Zhang will hold a banquet in the next few days to welcome them. The issue of Jin Army salaries will be fully decided after the Jin generals have a face-to-face discussion with Zhang. (April 10)

Fire at Shenyang First Institute of Technology

Total Loss Estimated at 400,000

Shenyang Dispatch: A fire broke out at the provincial First Institute of Technology, west of Fengyutan, in Shenyang on April 11, burning down dozens of questions in the front building and killing one firefighter. The reporter went to investigate the situation as follows: At 8:00 AM on the 11th, when the students of the First Institute of Technology were in the first class, the yamen servant suddenly saw that the chimney caught fire and spread to the reed shed. The workers in the shed ran outside, and when they got outside, they saw that the top of the two-story building was in flames. They immediately telegraphed the fire brigades in the provincial capital, the commercial port, and the chamber of commerce. At the same time, they telegraphed the Public Security Bureau of the provincial capital. After a while, Xiong Fei, the chief inspector of the Public Security Bureau, and Jiang Peihua, the inspector, led fifty members of the Public Security Team, and Wang Dashan, the head of the Fourth Branch of the provincial capital, led fifty members of the bureau and police, to the scene of the fire to maintain order. Thousands of nearby residents, both male and female, stood far away to watch. After about ten minutes, the fire brigades from various places arrived one after another to transport water and rescue, but the fire was too fierce to get close. At that time, Zhang, the captain of the fire brigade of the Public Security Bureau of the provincial capital, and Wang Tinglin, a member of the fourth team of the fire brigade of the Chamber of Commerce, bravely climbed the stairs. Unexpectedly, the top of the building collapsed, and the red light shot out. Zhang, the captain of the Public Security Fire Brigade, saw that the situation was not good and jumped down from the second floor. Wang Tinglin, a member of the Chamber of Commerce Fire Brigade, was lost in the fire and fell into the fire pit. When his colleagues worked together to rescue him, he had been charred. His thighs and head were completely burned away, leaving only his body, which was unbearable to see. By 10:00 AM, the fire was getting worse and worse. Twenty-eight classrooms and libraries in the front building were completely burned down. The Provincial Party Department, which was next door to the school on the south, sent many people to guard, and prepared water dragons and fire-fighting equipment, with strict precautions. Nearby neighbors also went to the roof to guard. The fire brigade of the Japanese station and the fire brigade of the Arsenal, and the sprinkling trucks of the Municipal Office, heard the news and mobilized all of them to come to help with the rescue. When the fire brigades from all sides were busy transporting water, unexpectedly, the water truck of the fire brigade of the Arsenal was driving south from Deyuanzhan Hutong, and the water truck of the Chamber of Commerce was driving from the north, causing the two trucks to collide. Yan Youde, the driver of the fire truck of the Arsenal, broke his left leg, and the driver of the Chamber of Commerce Fire Brigade was also injured in the arm. The water truck was damaged, and the crowd pushed it away and sent the two injured people to the Red Cross Hospital for treatment. By 12:00 noon, the fire had subsided slightly. All relevant parties in the provincial city came to the scene of the fire to monitor. Fortunately, all the students of the school escaped and no one was injured. According to the school's workers, the school building was built more than 20 years ago, and the project was purely old-fashioned. The chimney had been in disrepair for a long time, and smoke and fire spread to the roof of the library. The neighboring room was a chemical laboratory, which contained flammable drugs, so it exploded. According to the school's professors, the total loss is estimated at 400,000 yuan. By 6:00 PM, the embers had not been extinguished, and the fire brigades were still continuing to work hard to extinguish the fire. (April 11)

Election of National Assembly Representatives in Hankou

Voting Will Be Divided into Fourteen Locations on the 13th

Hankou Dispatch: For the election of National Assembly representatives in Hankou, the office previously stipulated that various groups would vote for three days, from the 13th to the 15th, and designated 14 election venues, and assigned chairmen and instructors to each election venue. At 8:00 AM on the 13th, the election venues were officially opened for voting. A total of more than 40 groups and more than 20,000 voters came to sign and vote in designated venues in order. The order of each venue was maintained by the police of each office, together with the security team of the Public Security Bureau. Election supervisor Liu Wendao, general manager Yang Zaichun, and officers He Fuzhou, Bi Weiru, Yang Hongzao, and Huang Jiwei went to inspect each venue separately. When Liu inspected the ninth work school election venue and the Li Da dance hall, he found that there was a situation of forced writing of ballots on behalf of others, and ordered the police to arrest them and escort them to the municipal government. He immediately reassigned Xu Yanchun and Ye Hongzhou as chairmen of the venue, and at the same time notified the chairmen of each venue to go to the government for training at 7:00 PM. Liu reported on the fraudulent situation he discovered and encouraged all officers to handle the matter seriously. It was not until 9:00 PM that the meeting ended. Elections will continue on the 14th and will not be completed until the 15th. (April 13)

Local Correspondence

Qingpu

A Bandit Police Engaged in Fierce Battle in Ren Deng Village, a Township Under the Jurisdiction of This County: Ren Deng Village, in the fourth district of this county, has been repeatedly subjected to kidnappings, and many people have been abducted and ransomed for huge sums of money. To date, several people have not been redeemed. The other day, a bandit ship was traveling in the nearby lake. A patrol boat of a certain number was passing by and saw that its movements were suspicious. It ordered the ship to stop for inspection, resulting in an exchange of fire between the two sides. After a long and fierce battle, the bandits were unable to resist and scattered in all directions.

The Chief of the Water Police Detachment is Accused of Dismissal: Yu, the chief of the Second Detachment of the First Squadron of the Water Police under the Provincial Public Security Force stationed in Fangjia Yao, 12th District, was accused by the town government of the town of multiple misdeeds and was dismissed. Li Jianzhang was appointed to fill the vacancy.

Chuansha

An Apprentice Attempts to Harm His Employer: Feng Honggen, an apprentice at Gu Taixiang Clock and Watch and Tooth Inlay Shop on Shipi Street in the city, is from Danyang and is 19 years old this year. During the past week, he stole a piece of gold from the store, sold it, and spent the money. Later, the owner of the store, Gu Chunming, found out and also found that the apprentice had stolen clocks and watches, etc. He immediately reprimanded him, hoping that he would repent. Unexpectedly, on the morning of the 9th, the apprentice poured nitric acid into his employer’s hot water bottle in an attempt to harm him. Fortunately, the owner of the store noticed it and was not poisoned. He then reported to the police and had the apprentice Feng Honggen detained and sent to the Public Security Bureau for investigation. After learning about the situation, he was sent to the county government on the 12th for punishment.

Songjiang

Two University Joint Survey Teams Arrive in Songjiang: The Education Colleges of National Central University and Jinan University, together with the Education Bureau of this county, formed the Songjiang County Education Survey Committee. More than 20 members of the entire team, led by professors Tai Shuangqiu, Cheng Zhichou, and Xie Xunchu from the two universities, arrived in Songjiang at 5:00 PM on the 13th. Starting today, they will begin various survey tasks, such as the school's situation, funding sources, professor training, school administration, and social situation, etc., and conduct surveys in groups. It is reported that the delay will be about one week.

The First District is Preparing for Literacy Promotion: The First District Office, under orders to hold a Literacy Movement Promotion Week today (the 14th), convened various agencies, public organizations, and schools to hold a preparatory meeting to discuss and decide that a promotion meeting will be held at the public sports field at 8:00 AM on the 21st of this month. The county government, the county party headquarters, the Education Bureau, the Public Security Bureau, and the First District Office were elected as the presidium. The county high school was also appointed as the director of the segmented speech, and it convened various secondary schools to allocate the segmented speech matters. The People's Education Center was appointed as the director of the performance and entertainment. Performances will be held at the Yue Temple People's Library at 1:00 PM that afternoon. It was also agreed that the district office should instruct the township heads to convene neighborhood leaders to conduct door-to-door persuasion and register.

Kunshan

A Carpenter's Wife Abducts and Hides a Maidservant: Chun'e, a maidservant from the home of Zhou Yunchao on Baihua Street, previously stole clothes and silver dollars and fled. He immediately searched for her everywhere and reported it to the Public Security Bureau for investigation. After an investigation by the investigation team on the 12th, she was found at the home of Xu A-huo, a carpenter who opened a woodworking shop on County West Street, and the stolen goods were recovered. It was then learned that the maidservant was abducted and hidden by A-huo’s wife, Ms. Sha, with the intention of selling them in other ports. Ms. Sha and Chun'e were escorted to the Public Security Bureau together with the original stolen goods and then sent to the county government for handling.

Refugees from Lujia Rob as They Leave the City: At 4:00 PM on the 12th, more than 300 refugees from Jiangbei suddenly arrived in Lujiaqiao Town, which is ten miles away from the city. Without asking for any reason, they rushed into the homes of villagers near the town to rob. Because of the large number of people, the villagers dared not resist. The town head telegraphed the county government to send police to drive them away. The losses suffered by the villagers were considerable.

Suzhou

The Chamber of Commerce Mediates a Fish Industry Dispute: The Suzhou fish industry and more than 3,000 fishmongers had a dispute over the change of old regulations in various industries, changing the cash code to a foreign code. Both parties petitioned the county government for relief. The county government instructed the county chamber of commerce to mediate. The county chamber of commerce convened a mediation meeting on the 14th. The representatives of the fish industry, Feng Jinkun and Lu Bohe, the representatives of the fishmongers, Zhu Zhifu and Gong Xibo, and the representatives of the chamber of commerce, Shi Junqing, Zhang Yipeng, and Song You attended. After a long discussion, three points were summarized: (1) Permission to change the foreign code and appropriately increase the bonus; (2) Still use the cash code, and the remaining balance will be calculated in foreign code; (3) The foreign code will be implemented after the Dragon Boat Festival. Both parties will respond to the Chamber of Commerce within three days, and then hold a second mediation meeting.

The Magistrate of Jiuyang County is Accused: Sun Yubo and others from Siyang County filed a complaint with the Procuratorate of the High Court, accusing the former Magistrate of Siyang County of protecting opium planting, violating the law, and neglecting his duties. They requested that the matter be investigated and dealt with according to law. After receiving the complaint, the High Procuratorate immediately ordered the Qingjiang Higher First Branch Court Procuratorate to investigate and verify the matter. The High First Branch Court Procuratorate has already replied yesterday (the 13th).

Wuxi

A Silk Factory Apprentice Attempts Suicide Twice and is Rescued: Qian Bogen, an apprentice at the Yuanfeng Silk Factory outside the store under the North Xinqiao in Zhoushanbang in this county, had previously deposited 460 yuan of his share money in the factory for interest. When his mother died on September 15th of last year, he paid 60 yuan of his deposit to the factory manager Hua Budan. By October, the silk industry had taken a sharp turn for the worse, and the factory also closed down, and lawyer Wu Yintang was hired to announce the liquidation. Qian Bogen went to withdraw his deposit, but Hua Budan repeatedly made excuses to postpone it. In anger, Bogen had suicidal thoughts and swallowed ten boxes of red phosphorus at Hua's house in an attempt to end his life. The Hua family noticed it and sent him to the Brothers Hospital for treatment, where he was rescued. Recently, Hua Budan went to the hospital to ask Bogen to pay the 5 yuan treatment fee, but failed. He then sent Qian to the Public Security Second Branch Bureau in charge. The Branch Bureau Chief refused to deal with it on the grounds of debt disputes. Later, Xu Ruirong sent Qian to the hospital for recuperation. After Bogen was admitted to the hospital, he took advantage of the lack of attention yesterday morning and swallowed phosphorus matches for the second time. Fortunately, he was spotted and stopped by a patient in the Zhou room, and no accident occurred. Qian's wife, Ms. Wang, is now looking for Budan to negotiate with him. It is unknown how it will be resolved.

A Stationery Shop's Adopted Daughter-in-Law Runs Away with Goods: Zhou Langfu, the owner of Zhou Deyuantang Stationery Shop near Shuyuan Lane in the north gate of this county, is 67 years old and is quite wealthy. He had a son in his later years. In order to entertain his old age, he adopted Zhu Rongxiu (18 years old), the daughter of Zhu Xiaoqing, who opened a shoe shop in front of the new county seven years ago, as his adopted daughter-in-law. After she entered the family, she got along well with her fiancé, Zhou Dayuan (16 years old). Recently, Rongxiu suddenly had an affair with Xu Peisheng, a clerk at the Wantai Chang Southern Goods Store in Ximen. They were secretly coming and going, like husband and wife. Peisheng felt that this situation could not last long and secretly agreed with Rongxiu to run away with the goods. Later, Rongxiu entrusted lawyer Yang Shi to publish a statement in the newspaper to terminate her marriage contract with the Zhou family. The Zhou family filed a lawsuit with the county court. Yesterday, the court summoned them, and the trial was opened. The plaintiff Zhou Langfu, Zhu Xiaoqing, and the defendants Zhu Rongxiu and Zhang Tangao all appeared in court. As a result, the court ordered the plaintiff to withdraw the case, ordered the defendant Zhang Zhigao to provide bail, and detained Zhu Rongxiu, pending the arrest of Xu Peisheng for further investigation.

The Thugs Who Beat the Police and Robbed Weapons are Arrested: The Public Security Fourteenth Branch Bureau in the Seventeenth District (Fuan Township) of this county was investigating a gambling case in the territory a month ago. Unexpectedly, the gamblers relied on their numbers and acted violently, resisting arrest and robbing weapons, and injuring the police officers. Afterwards, the branch bureau chief, Xun Dexing, reported to the County Public Security Bureau and sent detective captain Xue Furui to lead the police to the countryside to order the arrest and prosecution of the main offenders in this case, Kuang Renjin, Qian Yaomao, and others. Captain Xue received the order and led the officers yesterday to arrest the thug Kuang Renjin and escort him to the case. The other criminals have all fled.

The Collapse of a House in Shijia Field Causes Deaths and Injuries: The home of Shi Honglang in Shijia Field, west of Puhui Bridge outside the north gate, was almost completely burned down by a neighbor's carelessness last month. The other day, he collected a sum of money from relatives and friends to build three tile houses, which have been completed. Unexpectedly, his cousin Shi Ganxiong, who lives opposite, dug away the foundation of the wall yesterday (the 13th) due to a housing dispute. At about 4:00 PM, Qian Quankun, Shi Honglang's brother-in-law, ordered the tenant Qian Shunpei to bring earth bricks. However, in the room, with a loud bang, the house collapsed, crushing Qian Shunpei to death. Honglang's mother-in-law, Shi, and a two-year-old girl were also seriously injured. They were rescued by neighbors and reported to the First Branch Bureau of Public Security. Shi Ganxiong was detained and sent to the county. Today (the 14th), Wu, the trial judge, and Cao, the coroner, went to inspect and will handle the matter further.

Caozhuang Town Suffers Another Bandit Robbery: The shops in Caozhuang Town, Jiaxing, were robbed by bandits last year. Afterwards, follow-up work was carried out and the shops were ordered to continue operating. Unexpectedly, the vitality has not been fully restored. At more than 4:00 PM on the 13th, five more bandit ships arrived in the town, with more than 30 bandits on board, carrying spears, rifles, and white langlin guns. They robbed all the shops in the town at will and left in a rage at about 6:00 PM. When the bandits left, they also kidnapped five people, including Zhang Rongfeng. When the authorities in the city learned of this, they ordered the water and land police to rush to pursue them, but the bandits were nowhere to be found.

Verdict on the Water Police Squad Leader's Extortion Case: Zhang Hengen, a farmer from Wangjiangjing, Jiaxing, accused Wu Wenhua, the squad leader of the First Squad of the Seventh Team of the Water Police stationed in Wuyao, Jiashan, Xu Junxuan, the patrol leader, and other police officers of extorting money on various pretexts. The team leader in charge investigated and verified the matter and sent the seven suspects to the court for investigation. It is now known that the court has ordered the summons of witnesses for interrogation many times and announced the verdict the other day. Wu Wenhua, the squad leader of the First Squad, and Xu Junxuan, the patrol leader, were found guilty of extortion and were each sentenced to eight months in prison. The other five police officers and water patrols were all acquitted.

Education News

Important News

The Zhejiang Provincial Government Orders the Finance Department to Expedite the Allocation of Arrears to Various Middle Schools

The funding for various provincial middle schools in Zhejiang Province has been in arrears for four months, which has made it impossible to carry out school facilities and even impossible to maintain the lives of teachers and staff. A few days ago, the teachers and staff of various middle schools specially dispatched representatives Shi Bohou, Zhu Husheng and other 14 people to ask for help in the province and submitted a document to the provincial government, requesting that the arrears be paid off as soon as possible. After receiving the report, the provincial government, in addition to the instructions, has transferred the order to the Finance Department to expedite the allocation.

Zhejiang Province is Unable to Bear the Expenses of Zhejiang University

The Provincial Government Still Requests the Ministry of Finance to Allocate Funds

The Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Education previously agreed that, starting in March, the National Treasury would temporarily allocate 30,000 yuan per month to Zhejiang University, and the shortfall would be allocated by the province. Once the business tax is launched, the full amount will be offset by the business tax, as reported in this newspaper. It is now learned that the Zhejiang Finance Department stated that the business tax is entirely a local tax of the province. After the tax is levied in the future, the revenue tax will be used to offset the loss of the abolished Likin tax, which is a huge difference, and there is really no surplus to bear the expenses. It has requested instructions from the provincial government. The provincial government has transferred the situation to the Ministry of Finance, and the university’s expenses will still be fully allocated by the Central Government.

It is also reported that the student representatives of Zhejiang University, Yu Xitao, Hao Yanti, Li Hesheng, and others, petitioned the provincial government yesterday (the 14th) for funding issues.

Decision of the Anhui Provincial Government

After Yang Lianggong, the president of Anhui University, resigned, the Anhui Provincial Government had discussed and decided that during Yang's sick leave, the school affairs would be temporarily taken over by Ding Xuxian, the dean of the College of Science. Shanghai County's Literacy Movement Promotion Week Measures

After the Provincial Capital confirmed that the Literacy Movement Promotion Week in this county would be held from the 20th to the 26th of this month, the County Literacy Movement Promotion Committee actively prepared for it. It is now learned that the committee decided on the measures for all matters related to the promotion week at a temporary meeting yesterday. The details are extracted as follows:

County Association's Promotion Week Work Procedures: The County Association's opening ceremony will be held in Zhuanqiao Town on the afternoon of April 20th. On April 21st, it will participate in the speeches and entertainment of the District Branch in the Second District (Tangwan). On April 22nd, it will participate in the speeches and entertainment of the District Branch in the Third District (Beiqiao). On April 23rd, it will participate in the speeches and entertainment of the District Branch in the Sixth District (Maqiao). On April 24th, it will participate in the speeches and entertainment of the District Branch in the First District (Minhang). On April 25th, it will participate in the speeches and entertainment of the District Branch in the Fifth District (Chenhang). On April 26th, it will participate in the speeches and entertainment of the District Branch in the Fourth District (Sanlin).

District Branch's Promotion Week Work Procedures: (1) Post prohibitions and pictures widely in various villages one day before the opening ceremony. The publicity materials will be collected from the County Association. (2) Hold an opening ceremony on the first day and distribute publicity materials. (3) On the second day, the District Branch will hold a parade in conjunction with various agencies. (4) Hold a public speech and entertainment on the third day (the County Association will participate in the district). (5) Hold speeches and exhortations on the fourth, fifth, and sixth days (each school will organize a speech team to promote literacy in the nearby villages).

Goals of Promotion: (1) To arouse public attention to literacy. (2) To make the public understand the relationship between literacy and personal life, family happiness, social economy, local autonomy, national status, and human culture. (3) To make literate people understand the obligation to promote literacy education. Whether it is school students, agencies, organizations, industrial and commercial circles, staff, rural farmers, they can all be responsible for popularizing literacy education in their families and extend it to their neighborhoods and villages, or subsidize or contribute to literacy education.

Agencies and Organizations Participating in Promotion Week: (Opening Ceremony of the County Association) County Party Headquarters, County Government, County Bureaus, Representatives of Various Districts, Social Education Agencies, Zhuanqiao Elementary School, Beiqiao Elementary School, Township Governments near Zhuanqiao) First District) District Office of the Party Headquarters, Rural Teachers, Junior High School, Central Elementary School, People's Education Center, Township Governments in this District, Various Agencies and Organizations, (Second District) District Office of the Party Headquarters, Tangwan Elementary School, Central Tea Garden, Township Governments in this District, Various Agencies and Organizations, (Third District) Party Headquarters, District Office, Beiqiao Elementary School, Agricultural Education Center, Central Tea Garden, Township Governments in this District, Various Agencies and Organizations, (Fourth District) (Fifth District) (Sixth District) The participants are all similar, so they are not listed.

Shanghai Secondary School Basketball Tournament: Shanghai Jiangwan College Wins the Championship

丨56 to 31丨

Shanghai Middle School and Guanghua Make-up Game Not Completed

Yesterday, the Shanghai Jiangwan College High School basketball team defeated the powerful Jinan High School basketball team with a score of 56 to 31, and won this year's Shanghai Secondary School Sports Association basketball championship. How glorious! The referee was Zhang Guoxun. In the morning, Shanghai Jiangwan College led 27 to 16.

Conquering All Heroes and Becoming the Overlord

Qian Jingyong, the left forward of the Shanghai Jiangwan College High School basketball team, is an outstanding talent who has risen in the ranks. His shooting is as accurate as shooting a willow leaf from a hundred paces away. Feng Nianhua, the right forward, is as light as a swallow. He uses both left and right hands with ease. Li Ruchun, the center forward, is tall and upright, and excels in both guarding and shooting. Lu Zhonghui, the right guard, has a family background and is extraordinary. Sun Baoqing, the left guard, is capable in both offense and defense, a leader among them. Others, such as Huang Xinmin, Wang Gongying, and Dai Zu'en, are all top-notch talents. With such talents, coupled with the guidance of expert Wang Jinpeng, they conquered all the middle schools in Shanghai and became the overlord.

Left Guard Sun Baoqing - 2 balls - 0 times - 0 times - 4

Total - 25 balls - 6 times - 8 times - 56

With the General Gone, They Succumbed to the Wind

Yesterday, Shanghai Middle School's last strong opponent was the brave and skilled Jinan. Although their talents were generally inferior, their fighting spirit was excellent. Unexpectedly, one minute into the game, team captain Cao Xuexian injured his finger and was unable to continue fighting. With his spirit gone, what could be done? In the confrontation, they were forced everywhere. However, Han Zhenyuan's throws and Yin Guiren's defense were also outstanding. Jinan Score Sheet

Position and Name - Shots Made - Free Throws Made - Fouls - Points

Right Guard Zhang Jiyuan - 1 ball - 1 time - 0 times - 3

Left Guard Yin Guiren - 2 balls - 1 time - 3 times - 5

Total - 14 balls - 3 times - 8 times - 31

In Deep Water and Scorching Fire, Nothing Could Be Done

There were more than 500 spectators, 19 of whom were Shanghai Jiangwan College students who came to cheer for the school team. As soon as the whistle blew, applause erupted from all sides, breaking the peaceful atmosphere and starting the great battle. In the center jump ball, Shanghai Jiangwan College's Sun Baoqing chased after the shadow, accidentally hitting Jinan's Cao Xuexian's hand. It turned to Yu Wencai, who scored and returned. Although Jinan opened the scoring, Cao Xuexian was injured and left the field, which was not worth the loss. In the next center jump, Shanghai Jiangwan College's Sun Baoqing made up for his mistake and tied the score. Jinan's Han Zhenyuan casually threw the ball, which went in and came out. The viewers felt sorry for him. Feng Nianhua raised his arm and scored another point for Shanghai Jiangwan College. At this time, Jinan's morale was very strong, but they could not penetrate deep into enemy territory. Yin Guiren had no choice but to make a long shot, which hit the mark, making the score 4 to 5 (Shanghai Jiangwan College leading). Shanghai Jiangwan College reorganized its lineup, and all five players rose up. Qian Jingyong cut through the lane, and Li Ruchun rose from under the basket, scoring two consecutive goals, and their momentum suddenly increased. After that, Jinan seemed to be trapped in deep water and scorching fire, unable to extricate themselves. In the first half, Shanghai Jiangwan College had 27 points, and Jinan had 16.

From the End of the Road, Another Realm

Re-energized, Jinan took the lead again. Within two minutes, Gan Zhenyuan threw the ball backhand and scored, and Yu Wencai shot in from afar. Hundreds of Shanghai Jiangwan College students were celebrating a smooth journey to success, but unexpectedly encountered danger halfway, which was about to capsize the ship, and were greatly shocked and looked around in horror. Shanghai Jiangwan College's athletes, with their mission, bravely took the lead. Li Ruchun's two goals and Qian Jingyong's one goal were quickly won. Then they turned their tears into laughter and were ecstatic. But Jinan's good times did not last long, and the good times did not return. Although everyone was striving for progress, the general trend had passed, and it was difficult to recover. In the last eight minutes, Shanghai Jiangwan College replaced its substitutes and was able to fight as desired. As a result, with a score of 56 to 29, Shanghai Jiangwan College won.

Yesterday's Football Friendly Match: Furen Lost to Jinan

The result was three to one

Spectators shouted out of order

丨Tomorrow, Furen Will Play Fudan丨

Yesterday afternoon at 4:00, the Furen University football team played a friendly match with the Jinan University football team at the Chinese Baseball Field. This was the third match since the team came south. Furen performed very well, scoring one goal against Jinan first, but soon lost two penalty kicks in a row, and as a result, lost with a score of one to three. There were very few spectators yesterday, and some of them scolded and shouted, and attacked the referees, which was very abnormal and should be corrected. The summary of the situation is as follows:

Jinan University Lineup

Liang Shutang, Chen Bingxiang (Above)

Feng Yunyou, Fu Hexuan

Jiang Zongjin, Chen Jiaqiu (Above), Yang Baosen (Below)

Xie Quanhe, Lin Songfa (Below), Dai Linjing

Yang Baosen (Above), Chen Zhenhe

Chen Jiaqiu (Below), Tong Rongwen

Furen University Lineup

Wang Yumin, Cui Yongxi, Dong Shizuo, Cai Zhanyun, Tang Guo, Li Fenglou

Ye Delu, Fang Gechun (Above), Zhu Fuxiang (Below), Li Hongye, Cao Yu, Zhang Zhizhen

Jinan's Generals Were Not All Present

Jinan's lineup, in the first half yesterday, was unusually weak. Defender Jiang Shanjing did not come, and Mei Bao and Luo Haiguang were also injured and did not come. Lin Songfa did not arrive until the second half, and the situation turned around. Yang Baosen's right forward was extremely weak and incompetent, like a breach in the river embankment, with the flood flowing continuously from here. Jiang Shanjing was also absent, so Furen was attacked repeatedly in the first half. In the second half, Chen Jiaqiu changed to Yang's position, and the leakage was blocked. The performance of the forwards was mediocre. The only ones worth watching were Dai Linjing and Chen Zhenhe.

Furen's Loss Was Not Bad

Furen's performance was very good, and the spectators praised them. It is no wonder that some people roared and shouted injustice for Furen's defeat. Although Furen's defeat was due to their own carelessness, the forwards connected very well, the center back was strong, the goalkeeper was also steady, and the defenders were the weakest point. There were many goals conceded, and the two penalty kicks were very obvious fouls. Otherwise, even if they could not beat Jinan, they could still draw. Looking at the whole team's skills, it can be said that they were not bad.

Furen Scored First

Referee Zhou Jiaqi blew the whistle to start the game. At first, Furen's momentum was unstoppable, and Jinan was in danger, which led to exhaustion. Jinan kicked off, and Furen's Zhang Zhizhen intercepted it and sent it forward. Ye Delu made a backhand kick, and the five forwards advanced together. Cao Yu shot, and Jiang Zongjin patted it out. Ye Delu passed it to the center, and Tang Guoliang caught up and shot from afar, but it was not far off. Afterwards, Furen was very good, attacking fiercely. Jinan took the opportunity to counterattack, but Dai and Chen were weak and achieved nothing. Twenty minutes into the game, Zhang Zhizhen advanced rapidly from the right, and the inside was empty. Feng Yunyou went to stop him, but had no choice but to deflect it into a corner kick. Zhang Zhizhen took the kick, circled three or four times, and Fang Gechun headed it. Jiang Zongjin jumped up and pounced on it, and center forward Li Hongye kicked it in. Furen then took the lead.

Two Penalty Kicks

In less than five minutes, Furen suddenly faced a major disaster. Fu Hexuan dribbled the ball and advanced fiercely. There was no one in front of Furen's goal. Dong Shizuo rushed to save it, but was too hasty and accidentally pushed Fu to the ground. So a penalty kick was awarded. Dai Zhongpu kicked it, right in the center of the goal. Wang Yumin pounced on it but missed it, and it became a 1-1 tie. Misfortunes never come singly, and Furen lost another penalty kick. At that time, Dai Linjing, Chen Zhenhe, and Dong Rongwen advanced together, and their troops reached the gate. Cui Yongxi came to save it, and his hand bounced up, hitting his hand. Dai Linjing shot the second penalty, and the ball went down and then up again. In the first half, Jinan took the lead with a score of 2-1. In the second half, Jinan added Lin Songfa, and their military strength was very stable. Fifteen minutes into the game, Dai, the center forward, made a fierce kick, accurate and powerful, and broke through the enemy's gate again. Jinan finally won with a score of 3-1.

Spectators Shouted Out of Order

Yesterday, some spectators, because Furen was penalized two penalty kicks in a row, shouted loudly and attacked the referees, and some even scolded loudly, which was very inappropriate. Penalties for violations are clearly stipulated and cannot be faked. Moreover, sports emphasize spirit, followed by winning or losing, and then friendship. Victory or defeat is harmless. The extremely harmonious spirit of the two teams, if misunderstood by a shout, then the shouter's love is enough to harm them. Spectators are not sports experts, and should not lightly add unfounded evaluations. I hope that in the future, they will be strictly reformed.

Tomorrow, Fight the Fudan Team

Tomorrow afternoon, Furen will have a farewell battle with Fudan University. The location is in Jiangwan.

Free Talk

World News Briefs

— Haike

▲ A British lady is addicted to dogs. She keeps many dogs at home, all Pekingese. Each dog is given a house to live in and provided with all kinds of toys to play with. She treats them like her own children.

▲ According to a health expert in the United States, children who drink a glass of milk every day surpass those who do not drink milk in both intellectual and physical education. They are taller, weigh more, and their grades in school are also better.

▲ Several planters in Liverpool, England, have conducted planting experiments. It is said that some plants grow faster in moonlight than in sunlight, and the germination of seeds is also faster.

▲ A chapel in St. John's Wood, London, has been empty for twelve years without anyone entering it. Recently, it was bought by a famous sculptor who invested in turning it into a residence and sculpture workshop.

▲ A French woman was awarded a military medal by the government in 1859 for assisting wounded soldiers in the Battle of Solferino in Lombardy. She died in May 1923 at the age of ninety-two.

A Sad Record of the Public Memorial for Hu Liseng

— Sun Choucheng

The 10th of this month marked the sixth anniversary of the passing of revolutionary elder Hu Liseng. Yu Youren, President of the Control Yuan, Zhang Qun, Mayor of Shanghai, as well as important figures in the party and state, old friends of Hu Gong, Zhang Puquan, Yin Zhufu, Li Genyuan, etc., recalling Hu Gong's revolutionary achievements, jointly initiated a public memorial at Wusheng Zen Temple on Chongqing Road and Montauban Road to express their condolences. Hu Gong joined the Tongmenghui at the age of seventeen and dedicated himself to the revolution, and was known for his bravery. Choucheng admired him and went there in the rain. What I saw is recorded below to express my sorrow.

On that day, the gate of the temple was hung with an eleven-character bamboo cloth banner reading (Memorial Hall for Mr. Hu Liseng's Sixth Anniversary). The ink was fading due to wind and rain. In the auditorium, a lake-colored silk streamer donated by Yu Youren was hung in the center, inlaid with the four large characters (The Spirit Returns to Mount Hua). On the side was a mourning couplet sent by Zhang Yuejun, which read (Thinking of the style for six years, how many times has the Central Plains changed); (A century of agreement, great achievements will remain between heaven and earth). On the table was a yellow paper spirit tablet, about one foot long and five inches wide, with red paper inlaid at the top and bottom, painted with golden lotus flowers and inlaid with the four characters (Buddha's Light Shines Everywhere). Below was written the phrase (Position of the late General Hu Gong Liseng). In front of the tablet were eight large and four small vegetarian dishes, and a cup of tea and rice each. There were also eight high-footed basins, each containing four kinds of fruits and dried snacks. Incense and candles stood side by side. Under the table were two large flower wreaths, with the names of Lin Shi, Ji Liang, and Si Zi tied on the wreaths. A name card of Zhang Qun, the mayor of Shanghai, was hung on one of them. In the side room, tea and snacks were provided on the left for the guests to rest. On the right was a registration desk, manned by staff. Because the initiators were far away in Pingjing, Suzhou, Hangzhou and other places, not many people came. It was heard that the arrangement of the venue was undertaken by Chen Zhishuo. When Hu Gong was the governor of Henan, Chen was the director of the Department of Finance and had a deep friendship with him, so he described Hu Gong's deeds in great detail that day. It was said that Gong was from Fuping, Shaanxi. He lost his parents at a young age and was raised by his grandmother. He had great ambitions and was angry at the corruption of the Qing government. In the first year of Xuantong, he joined the Tongmenghui and united with comrades in Weinan to plan a major uprising. After the Wuchang Uprising in Xinhai, Gong served as the commander of the New Army, responding in Shaanxi. He was only just over twenty years old at the time. After the success, he voluntarily resigned and went to Japan to study. In the second year of the Republic of China, he returned to China and was elected as the commander of the expedition to Mongolia. The matter was blocked and not realized. He then went to Japan to see the Premier and made detailed plans for military affairs, entrusting him with the affairs of Shaanxi. After returning to China, he made many remarkable achievements. He died of illness at the age of only thirty-four. Hearing this, I was moved. On that day, because Hu Gong's relatives and friends were few, there was no emphasis on formality during the public memorial. Everyone came and paid their respects as they arrived. Mayor Zhang arrived at the meeting at three o'clock in the rain, wearing a suit and a cloak. He took off his cloak at the entrance and bowed three times to the spirit tablet, with a look of concern on his face. He mentioned that there were not many mourners and sighed frequently at the desolation, and wished to take on the expenses of today alone. Among the elegiac couplets, the one written by Li Yinquan was the most poignant, which read (Feeling the past for six long years, the world is difficult and you have gone); (Returning to God beyond the three realms, I am ashamed of the loss of my close friends). It is said that Mr. Li has been living in seclusion in Wumen, studying Buddhism and not asking about worldly affairs for several years. In recent years, his relatives and friends have passed away, and he has been sighing about it. He was deeply moved by the commemoration of the sixth anniversary of the death of his old friend.

A Warning to Those Who Commit Suicide

— Qingqu

Since people are born, who can avoid death? Therefore, from the moment they are born, they will eventually return to emptiness. Death is not necessarily to be mourned, and it is not worth mourning. Buddhists speak of Nirvana, Liezi speaks of the benevolent resting, and the unworthy hiding. Our Mengsou said that dying is also being born. Jia Yi said that life is floating and death is resting. Therefore, those who are born into the world, and can rise above all creatures, even if they live to be a hundred years old, and are still mediocre, living a life of drunkenness and death, leaving behind this stinking skin bag, only to pollute the heavens and the earth, are also fortunate to be born. Our late teacher Confucius called them thieves. The reason for condemning them is deep.

Some Europeans hold the principle of sacrifice, saying that the world cannot be saved without promoting the Stoic school. Our Confucian school also has the saying of hearing the Tao in the morning and dying in the evening. It can be said that they arrive at the same destination by different paths. However, humans are living beings, and death is not reversible. If one has not experienced the world for long, and abandons the golden years with a youthful qualification, just to close one's eyes and decide to leave oneself in order to end it all, then even if one gets rid of the physical body and preserves the soul, what benefit is there in the end, even if the heart does not die, while the body is dead?

Our country is worried about the lack of talent in recent times, and is relying on outstanding talents of the younger generation to emerge in time and become a crystal light. But they do not consolidate themselves, forget their original intentions, and willingly sink into a long death, suddenly disappearing without a trace. Is there any difference between rotting with plants and trees and perishing together? Is it really that sorrow can hurt people and cannot be waited for a moment? Now, the changes in the emotional world are commonplace, and the waves of the sea of desire are never stable. Those who turn clouds and overturn rain constantly change their minds. They are everywhere you look. In the morning, they are phoenixes, and in the evening, they turn into owls. To cross the river of love and transcend the sea of hatred is not something that the mediocre can hope for. Therefore, know that human troubles come with our lives. Even in extremely unfree situations, regard it as a place to endure hardships and repent. Otherwise, only be sad and depressed, and gain the words "death by love". How thin is this self-treatment?

Alas, suicides today, whether male or female, are mostly young people. To avoid this epidemic, I say that these three essentials should be understood. First, one must be enlightened in thought. Second, one must be dissolved in material things. Third, one must be aware in psychology. If one can understand these three and add the effort of overcoming them, then human happiness and perfect good fortune will be seen here. If we do not encourage each other, but only see the empty shadows of kindred spirits on the beautiful islands and shores, and the short-lived flowers of peaches and plums on the jade terraces, and still say that it is the environment that forces us, and the situation that does not allow us, and we have no choice but to apologize with death, do not know that this is still self-inflicted, and what is the blame on others? This is why I cannot but repeat my words to blame.

A Visit to Sheshan

— Chen Boying

Songjiang was anciently known as Yunjian, famous for its Nine Peaks and Three Mao Lakes. The Nine Peaks are Phoenix Mountain, Xue Mountain (i.e., Yu Ping Mountain), Sheshan, Chen Mountain (i.e., Shen Mountain, i.e., Xi Lin Mountain), She Mountain (i.e., She Gong Mountain), Ji Mountain, Heng Mountain (i.e., Hengyun Mountain), Tianma Mountain (i.e., Gan Mountain), and Kun Mountain (i.e., Xiao Kun Mountain). The mountains stand apart, like reclusive scholars in ceremonial robes, bowing to each other. Although they lack spectacular grandeur, their pure tranquility and delicate beauty have their own charm. Among them, Sheshan stands out for its beautiful scenery. Sheshan is twelve miles from both Songjiang County and Qingpu County, northeast of Lu Mountain and east of Shenshan Pond. It is eighty zhang high and eighteen li in circumference, surpassing other mountains in height and size. Legend has it that a person named She cultivated the Dao here and ascended to immortality, hence the name. During a spring vacation, I went there with a friend. We traveled by boat and, arriving at the foot of the mountain, disembarked. The mountain resembled embracing arms, forming a semi-circular shape, with a western and an eastern mountain. The western mountain has one peak, while the eastern mountain has two peaks. Entering from the western mountain, there are countless bamboos. The whispering bamboos and verdant bamboo groves cover the entire mountain. Further in, there is the Bixian Temple on the mountain. Following the path up, the main hall is long gone, only the side rooms remain, inscribed with "Qibi Mountain Cottage." The incense offerings are sparse and desolate. Descending and advancing further, we arrived at the gate of the Catholic Church. A statue of the Virgin Mary stands above the gate. Entering the gate and climbing the steps, we found the chapel halfway up the mountain. Looking down, there was a small lake shaped like an autumn leaf. Turning west, there were three small, scattered pavilions, each with a statue: one of Jesus holding a small child, one of Mary, and one of Jesus showing his sacred heart. Stepping back and further up, we came to the zigzag road. Trees were planted along both sides of the road. At each end of the road, a shrine was built, each enshrining stories of Jesus's crucifixion. There were fourteen shrines in total. The road led upwards, reaching the summit. At the top, a large cathedral was being built. Construction had been going on for seven or eight years but was not yet completed. The church foundation covered about an acre. All the foundations, pillars, and thresholds were made of stone, as smooth as a mirror, and various patterns were carved on them, combining solemnity, solidity, beauty, and unity. The scale of the project was unseen elsewhere. Inquiring of the workers, they said that it would take another two or three years to complete the roof. To the east, there was an astronomical observatory, where one could previously observe the moon. Now, the instruments had been moved to Xujiahui. Next to it was a pagoda, dilapidated and inaccessible, likely the Xiudaozhe Pagoda. At this point, the western mountain had been fully explored. It was midday, and we were hungry. So, we went down, settled under the awning of the boat, sat in a small skiff, and poured wine from our flasks. We also bought freshly unearthed bamboo shoots from a mountain family, cooked them in the stove, added a little soy sauce, and served them in large bowls. Everyone eagerly ate them, finishing them in an instant. The taste was extremely fresh and delicious, making us laugh at how bear paws and shark fins were merely overrated. After the meal, we climbed the eastern mountain. Looking around, the fields were arranged in rows, and the long river resembled a belt, widening our horizons. Descending, we walked west along the river. A huge rock protruded from the riverbank, where we could sit. The locals said that this was Chen Meigong's fishing rock. Across the river, there were several willow trees, their branches reflecting in the water like a net, with fish swimming in and out. Gazing at it for a long time, it was no less captivating than on the Hao River. In general, bamboo was the most abundant tree in the mountains, accounting for about eight out of ten. The other trees, such as cypress, elm, juniper, and ginkgo, accounted for only two out of ten. As for the Lingfeng Temple, West Temple, and East Temple built in the Song Dynasty, and the Zhaoqing Temple, Hui Ri Temple, and Xuan Miao Temple built in the Ming Dynasty, none of them remain today. Most of the mountain is now church property. I don't know who sold it at the time, which is regrettable. We sailed back at dusk. The companions on the trip were Gu Zaoying, Gu Zhi Zhou, the Gu Jinggao brothers, Cai Hui, Zhang Dezhai, and Fei Chenglai. I record this as a fleeting memory for the future.

▲ Correction: In yesterday's "Casual Talk on Seasonal Items" (3), the third line "(亦其一) is wrong, it should be (則甚易). The fourth line (繼後陰水) is wrong, it should be (纖微濾水). Also, in "Casual Talk on Seasonal Items" (4), the first character of the tenth line (納) is wrong, it should be (鈉). The first character of the sixteenth line (開窗) is wrong, it should be (聞雷). We correct these errors."

Lakezhou Travelogue (1)

— Shen Xingchu

Huzhou, also known as Wuxing, is a place where towering mountains compete in beauty, and jade waters connect to the sky. It possesses a natural, spiritual essence. The Yousheng Travel Group took advantage of the Western Qingming Festival holiday to travel together and thoroughly enjoy the scenic spots and historical sites. Here, I record a general account for future travelers to use as a reference.

This spring tour consisted of over six hundred people, led by Ni Ziyi. A special train was arranged to Hangzhou. Forty-three people, including the reporter Zhou Shoujuan from this newspaper, the painter Hu Boxiang, and the photographers Zhu Shouren and Guo Xiqi, also participated. We departed on a special train at 8:20 PM on April 2nd and arrived in Hangzhou at 1:00 AM. We stayed in various hotels near the train station.

On the 3rd, we rose at 5:00 AM, washed up, and finished breakfast. At 7:00 AM, we boarded two long-distance buses at the train station and set off. The journey from Hangzhou to Huzhou was ninety kilometers, and the bus took three hours to arrive. The local branch of our group, along with local dignitaries, led Boy Scouts and the orphanage military band to welcome us at the station. We arrived at the Central Hotel at 11:00 AM. After settling in, we had a late lunch at 4:00 PM. In the afternoon, we toured the scenic spots in the city, starting with

▲ Qian Garden: Commonly known as the Lu Family Garden, it was built by Lu Xinyuan in the Qing Dynasty. It was also where Dai Jitao studied. The Chinese fringetrees are dazzling. The Nine-Bend Bridge and rockeries are particularly ingenious. Next, we went to

▲ Lotus Manor: The villa of Zhao Zi'ang in the Yuan Dynasty. The scenery is beautiful and secluded. It is now the Yang Family Ancestral Hall. Crossing the river, we arrived at

▲ Shen Family Charitable Estate: The former gentleman Shen Jingxuan made a fortune exporting rice, so he established the charitable estate. His son further expanded its operations. It is surrounded by water on all sides, forming a natural setting, with a platform and the Five Old Men Stones, among other wonders. Then we arrived at

▲ Silk Weaving Guild: The plaque in the hall reads "Ancestor of Divine Craftsmanship." We drank tea and rested briefly, engaging in lively conversation with a mix of seriousness and humor. At 4:15 PM, we arrived at

▲ Yi Garden: Commonly known as the Ding Family Garden, it was founded by Ding Naiyang. It is filled with fine trees, rare flowers, bamboo fences, and flower paths, making it the best garden in Huzhou. The layout is particularly neat and luxurious. Ten large paintings of "A Hundred Beauties" by Qiu Shizhou hang on the walls, which are quite valuable. It is not usually open to the public, but our group had arranged in advance to feast our eyes. Afterwards, we went to

▲ Park: The park is well-laid out. Inside is the Moyao Pavilion, built by Prefect Sun Jue during the Xining era. Ancient writings and inscriptions from within the territory since the Han Dynasty are collected there for reference.

Indian Travelogue (24)

— Linghua

The weather turned cold at night, so I put on my Chinese cotton robe in the morning. The monks from Ceylon (Sri Lanka) who lived with me also caught colds. So did I. This is because the climate on the island of Ceylon is mild, unlike the variability of Jiacheng. I walked through the city and saw people draped in blankets, some yellow and some green. I thought these people were just carrying blankets home after buying them. But then I saw that many people were draped in blankets on their shoulders. I wondered why so many people were buying blankets, and why they were all draped on their shoulders. Upon closer inspection, everyone was draped in blankets. When I asked, I learned that this was Indian clothing. I was puzzled. One blanket is enough to cover oneself at night or to wear through the winter. But it is a pity that poor people on the streets are still wearing only a single layer of clothing, lying on the ground. It is truly pitiful. I have read the Biography of Faxian and know that those who promoted Buddhism in China were not only Indians, but also people from the island of Ceylon made great contributions to our country. Although Ceylon is an island, it occupies a superior position in cultural and transportation history. Therefore, I respect the Ceylon monks all the more and hope they will come to the East again to promote the Great Dharma. The Ceylon monk was reading a biography of Gandhi, the leader of the Indian independence movement, and urged me to read it. I felt that once I arrived in India, I was surrounded by Gandhi's aura. The Indians believe in him even more than they believe in Buddha. He is a person of faith who combines politics, economics, morality, and religion. It is important to study his outline and tell my countrymen.

On the 10th, I was a busy person and did not have time to read much. But Gandhi's biography was a thick volume of over five hundred and eighty Western pages. It was his autobiography translated into English by a student. I spent a day and night summarizing it as follows. Please pay attention to it, compatriots. Gandhi's autobiography does not need to be read. Just look at his photograph, and it is all clear at a glance. He looks like a beggar, with no clothes on top or bottom, just a loincloth around his waist. He can truly be called a true man. His appearance is also like a beggar, with not the slightest difference. Yet now he is the central leader of India's political, religious, and economic movements. Isn't that strange? In my opinion, the world's sages are often beggars. Buddha abandoned his throne to become a beggar. Jesus was not allowed to carry money and traveled from village to village. Socrates wandered barefoot. Gandhi is in their line, but he added a national movement, thus combining politics and religion into one. His autobiography is filled with Sanskrit words, which are not easy to read. The English name is The Story of My Experiments with Truth by Gandhi. India has four classes. The first is the clergy, the second is the king and officials, the third is merchants, and the fourth is farmers and workers. Gandhi belongs to the third class of people. His father was an experienced merchant but had no learning. His mother was a devout Hindu. Since childhood, Gandhi was influenced by his wet nurse, named Ramhan, who often recited the name of the god Rama.

Commercial News

Gold Market Approaching Swap Period

The gold market situation has recovered from yesterday's low. The benchmark price on the 14th recovered from its low, but there were no special changes in the situation. Throughout the day, there were only about five taels of fluctuations. No major buying or selling occurred among the various firms due to the approaching swap period. The morning market was slightly weak because the silver market had indeed reported a decline, but there were not many buyers, so people's confidence weakened. Afterwards, it rose and fell rapidly, hovering around 720 taels, with only two or three taels of turnover. As exchange bills, both official and unofficial, showed no prosperity, the market felt peaceful. However, as foreign exchange such as the rupee recovered, sellers in the market seemed active, and the market turned downward. Later, it was priced at 716-717 taels. This morning, the outlook is expected to be slightly higher.

The morning opened with a drop of 2.5 taels. The May contract opened with a decrease of 2.5 taels, at 719 taels. The broad market was only down by 1/16, while the price of silver fell by 1/4, and private telegrams were reduced by 1/4. The underlying support seemed strong, and various parties were unwilling to sell. Shortly after, it fell from 20 taels to 17.5 taels. When Hengxing and others sold, and British gold was being traded between various banks at 133.75 for June, and then Holland bought at 375, and Dadesheng, Tongtaichang, Cuichang, Yongchang, and others also came to buy, it rose by 4 taels to 21.8 taels at around 9:30. The British gold quotation remained unchanged, and some retail investors sold off, immediately reducing it by a small 2 taels to 19.5 taels. At times, it increased to 20.04 taels. However, the exchange market was very calm. Magalies quoted 3.125 for June, and Sumitomo offered Japanese gold at 1.59 taels, but sellers were active on the trading floor. Tongtaichang came out again, causing the price to drop by 4 taels. At 10:00, it was 16.5 taels. Then, Yongfeng and Yuanheng bought, and hedgers sold British gold. Huabi and Taiwan bought 375, so the price of gold increased by more than 4 taels. At 10:30, it was 21 taels. Subsequently, Yuanmao Yong and Guangbang sold again, falling back by 3 taels. At 11:00, it was 18 taels. Later, it went upwards as Wanxing, Shunli, Qianchang, and Xiang came to buy. After 11:30, it was priced at 20.03 taels. Physical gold was sold for hedging, and it fell back to 17 taels. By the afternoon close, it had been raised by one or two taels because Shunli and others continued to buy, to 18.5 taels. It was again about two taels higher on the trading floor. The quoted price was still 777 taels, down about 60 taels.

The result was a small decrease of 5 taels. The afternoon market opened at 19.5 taels. In an instant, the Indian exchange rate rose by a small two annas, and it immediately rose to 21 taels. Suddenly, Guangbang sold, and British gold was at 133.125, and banks were willing to sell, so it retreated to 19 taels. By 2:45, there seemed to be more buyers, and it increased slightly by 2 taels. By 3:30, it was 21.2 taels. Afterwards, the Indian exchange rate returned to a large one anna, immediately decreasing by 1 tael. By 4:00, selling pressure increased sharply, and Yongfeng, Longsheng, Yuanmao Yong, and others successively sold off. However, British gold and others had no changes. However, the consensus among the industry was downwards, causing the price to fall by more than 3 taels. The fluctuations were only about 1 tael in half an hour. By the close at 4:30, it was only 16.5 taels, a decrease of 5 taels compared to yesterday (the physical gold was raised by 5 taels). The highest price for the day was 20.8 taels, and the lowest price was 16.5 taels, a difference of 5.3 taels. The physical market opened at 20 taels in the morning, closed at 18.5 taels at noon, and was 19.5 taels in the afternoon, closing at 17 taels. The quoted price was down 56-57 taels to 60 taels. The registered price was 19 taels, with a water surcharge of 15 taels in the morning and 13 taels in the afternoon.

Most of the transactions were swap trades. Hengxing, Shengda, Yuanmao Yong, Yuantai, Futai, Heng, etc. all sold, while Yuanheng, Fuchang, Hengyu, Dadesheng, etc. all had receipts and payments in substantial amounts. Tongtaichang, Shunli, Wanxing, Fuyu, Zhifeng, Yongqian, Changxiang, Zhenchangxiang all bought in. Cuichang and Yong slightly sold off. The physical gold had very complex inflows and outflows. Dalianbang sold 800-900 bars and bought 500 bars.

Yarn and Cotton: Yarn Market Slightly Improving

The yarn market is slightly firm because raw cotton prices have increased, and sales of current yarn are gradually improving. Sales in North China are very smooth, and Sichuan merchants are also continuously buying. Therefore, the situation of current yarn is quite good, and there is hope for further development in all aspects. However, most people have a neutral attitude because there are still thick stocks of coarse yarn, so the selling price is difficult to raise. As for future yarn, they continue to short when prices rise, so the market situation is still loose and not tight at all. However, the major players have a firm attitude and have no intention of releasing their stocks. Even with good news, the market has not fully flourished. However, judging from the overall trend, there should be hope for an increase.

Human Mark Trending Higher: The human mark market opened with rising American cotton prices, and the current demand news was good, so the market atmosphere became tighter, and each mark rose by seven or eight qian. Cotton Market Progress

The cotton market is trending upwards because American and Indian cotton prices are rising, and exchange rates are still unfavorable for long positions. Japanese merchants are also shifting their focus to higher prices, resulting in a tighter market atmosphere with more buyers. However, cotton factories are showing signs of easing up on spot cotton purchases. Nevertheless, inventories across the board are low, and sentiment remains firm.

Han Piao [cotton standard] is rising with American cotton. The Han Piao market opened higher following foreign cotton trends, with firm prices. Prices for each month rose by twenty to thirty qian [Chinese monetary unit]. The market atmosphere was slightly calmer in the afternoon, with fluctuations of five fen [smaller Chinese monetary unit]. The total volume of transactions was 21,100 dan [unit of weight]. It was found that Shen Chang sold 1,800 dan, Chang Ji sold 700 dan, and Yuan Feng sold 900 dan. The purchases included Da Feng with 1,100 dan, Gong Tai with 1,000 dan, Heng Yi with 1,000 dan, and Chang Feng with 1,300 dan. The closing prices are recorded below:

Food　Rice Market Firm in the North, Steady in the South

In Zhabei [northern district of Shanghai] yesterday, over thirty ships arrived from inland. The special high-quality japonica rice [Geng] was rare and unaffected by market fluctuations. Ordinary medium-quality japonica rice sales continued actively, with many parties purchasing eagerly. Prices turned upward slightly, and the market gradually showed positive signs. Demand for thin [Bo] paddy rice was slow due to scarce supply, resulting in little trading and steady prices. Demand for Yang Xian rice [Indica] was mediocre, with only special grades showing firmness, while others barely maintained their original levels. Arrivals of Dubu Xian rice were slow to sell, with no upward or downward movement in the market. Arrivals of Bai Yuan [white round-grain rice] were met with sluggish wholesale and retail sales, resulting in overall market stability.

In Shanghai South [southern district of Shanghai] yesterday, around twenty ships arrived in the inner port. Sales in this district remained slow. Changshu and Suzhou machine-milled white japonica rice initially showed a shortage in the morning, but the market turned steady due to news of firmness from the north, resulting in no overall price changes. The southern paddy rice market was sluggish, with only a small amount selling, resulting in mediocre prices. Buying interest in Yang Mu Jian [Indica rice variety] remained quiet, with prices remaining high and steady, but with occasional cuts. The situation with Bai Yuan [rice variety] was still unfavorable, with demand remaining weak. Top-grade Bai Yuan opened at 11.30-11.40 yuan.

Northern Merchants Trialing Guest Rice [Ke Mi]

The market situation for guest indica rice [Ke Xian] remained active yesterday. In addition to Guangzhou merchants continuing their trials, merchants from northern areas such as Tianjin, encouraged by active grain sales in those regions, were also trialing shipments to the market. If transportation and sales prove profitable, they may continue shipments. Interest in guest yuan rice [Ke Yuan] was particularly strong. Northern merchants purchased 200 bags of Hunan machine-milled yuan rice at a price of 14.06 yuan, and 150 bags of Jiangxi machine-milled early rice at a price of 10.97 yuan. Guangzhou merchants purchased 71 bags of Jiangxi machine-milled late rice at a price of 11.22 yuan. Prices were similar to the previous market.

Label Flour Market: Short-term Lively, Long-term Steady

Yesterday's flour market, after opening in the morning and afternoon, showed a trend of being lively in the near-term but steady in the long-term. Quotations for foreign wheat were also better by 0.20 to 0.30 yuan. Overall, this naturally boosted confidence. However, due to different needs between near and forward delivery, there was some slight movement in response to the situation. Because customer sales for this month are still good, and the factories are now able to process current flour, most are adding 7.5 fen or 1 qian to the standard price. Therefore, the market atmosphere is naturally stable. The forward market has little buying or selling due to a lack of confidence, resulting in steady prices. However, if this month continues to be lively, the forward market may be boosted somewhat. As a result, this month was better by 1.25 fen compared to the previous day, May was 0.01 yuan better, June was unchanged, July was 0.025 yuan better, and August and September were unchanged.

Futures Wheat Market: Steady Situation

Yesterday's futures wheat market, after opening in the morning and afternoon, generally presented a steady situation. Because quotations for foreign wheat were again better by 0.20 to 0.30 yuan, those observing the situation tended to be stable. However, domestic merchants are observing that although wheat seedlings are weaker than in previous years, the season for new goods is approaching. With foreign wheat being imported in large quantities, factory use is not as high as in previous years, so most are observing, and buying interest is sluggish. As a result, this month did not open in the afternoon, but was better by 0.01 yuan in the morning. May was better by 0.02 yuan compared to the previous day, June, July, and August were better by 0.01 yuan, and September was slightly worse by 0.01 yuan.

Sugar Market: Raw Sugar and White Sugar Rise, Transactions Quiet

Unified-Brand Ice Sugar Opening Still Firm

Yesterday's sugar market telegrams from producing areas indicated that Cuban spot sugar remained unchanged. New York sugar futures for all months were up one point compared to the previous day. North-South Goods: Dried Peach Meat Scarce, Outlook Positive

Dried peach meat prices in Tianjin have been high recently, so there have been no arrivals. Although prices in Hankou are lower, spot prices are also not attractive. In addition, there are few goods en route. Based on current inventory levels, it will be difficult to meet new demand in the future, so prices are expected to rise. According to Hankou telegrams, the price is 41.6 taels, and after adding all external costs, it is higher than the Shanghai market. Yesterday's market price here was 45 taels, and the trend is stable.

Silk and Tea: Yellow and White Filature Prices Difficult to Sell

Yesterday, there was no improvement in the silk market in the sunning port for foreign firms. The exchange rate was tight, and overseas telegrams indicated that silk prices were declining. Although American firms were interested in yellow and white filatures, their opening prices were still low, and sales were difficult. Yesterday, only Qianli and others imported 50 bales of Shanghai white filatures, and Xinfu and others imported 17 bales of yellow filatures. Prices were generally weak.

Yuhang Starts Incubating Silkworm Eggs

The silkworm season in areas such as Yuhang and Linping in Zhejiang Province is earlier than in the Huzhou and Jiaxing areas. In previous years, eggs were incubated around the Qingming Festival, but this year, due to the cold weather, farmers in various cities and towns have only recently started incubating silkworm eggs. Most of the eggs being incubated are of the Yuhang variety, and they should all be hatched before the Grain Rain Festival.

Tea Merchants: Legal Sales of Zhen Mei [Precious Eyebrow tea] Slightly Active

Yesterday, foreign firms such as Jardine Matheson and Jinlong in the Zhen Mei green tea market received telegrams from legal sources indicating demand. As a result of continued negotiations, over 560 boxes were sold, at prices ranging from 48 to 55 taels. There were no major transactions for items such as Needle Eyebrow and Fine Eyebrow teas in the market yesterday. Sales of Keemun black tea were also quite sluggish.

Metals: Eastern White Iron Shortage, Prices Rise Sharply

Recently, transactions for eastern white iron have been booming like grass after rain. Purchases from the Yangtze River Road and merchants from inland areas are large, while imports are not large. Due to the supply-demand imbalance, confidence is strong, and the market shows promising signs. According to Osaka news in recent days, all goods produced by Japanese manufacturers have been purchased by India, resulting in tight Japanese news and a firmer market atmosphere. As a result, the market price rose by 0.03 to 0.04 yuan per sheet yesterday. A six-foot sheet was valued at 1.08 taels, and a seven-foot sheet was at 1.27 taels. There are still many buyers, and the market is expected to continue rising.

Currently, No. 24 sells for 15.75 taels, No. 26 for 16 taels, and No. 28 for 17 taels.

Company Iron Shortage, Prices Soar

Recently, there has been a shortage of 200-pound company iron, while purchases from various merchants have been exceptionally enthusiastic. As a result, supply cannot meet demand, confidence is unusually strong, and the market shows great promise. Prices have soared by 4 taels, and each case is valued at 35 taels.
